import csv
import os

def process_combined_csv(input_filename, output_filename):
    with open(input_filename, 'r') as infile, open(output_filename, 'w', newline='') as outfile:
        reader = csv.reader(infile)
        writer = csv.writer(outfile)
        
        # Write headers to the output CSV
        writer.writerow(['Date', 'Email', 'Event'])
        
        for row in reader:
            date, email, event = "", "", ""
            
            # Extract date, email, and event from the row
            for item in row:
                if is_valid_date(item):
                    date = item
                elif "@" in item:
                    email = item
                elif is_valid_event(item):
                    event = item
            
            # Print the extracted details for verification
            if date and email and event:
                print(f"Processed: Date: {date}, Email: {email}, Event: {event}")
                writer.writerow([date, email, event])
            else:
                print(f"Skipped: {row}")

def is_valid_date(s):
    return '/' in s and len(s.split("/")) == 3

def is_valid_event(s):
    return s in ['Opened', 'Accepted', 'Delivered', 'Clicked']

input_path = os.path.join('C:\\Users\\lorio\\OneDrive\\Documents\\Zensights\\Email Project', 'all_july_tables_combined.csv')
output_path = os.path.join('C:\\Users\\lorio\\OneDrive\\Documents\\Zensights\\Email Project', 'refined_output.csv')

process_combined_csv(input_path, output_path)
